       <article class="content-wrapper wrapper clearfix detail-block-md" id="article-34783">
        <header class="content-header">
         <h1>
          Terrifying Man Selling Dead Trees Out Of Middle School Parking Lot
         </h1>
        </header>
        <main class="content-body large-thing" data-area="Article Body">
         <div class="content-masthead">
          <figure class="content-image on-trigger-overlay">
           <div class="image" data-image-id="24501" data-type="image">
            <div>
            </div>
            <noscript>
             <img src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2450/1/16x9/600.jpg"/>
            </noscript>
           </div>
          </figure>
          <div class="on-overlay on-overlay-scale">
           <button class="on-overlay-close" type="button">
            Close
           </button>
           <figure class="content-image">
            <div class="image" data-image-id="24501" data-type="image">
             <div>
             </div>
             <noscript>
              <img src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2450/1/16x9/600.jpg"/>
             </noscript>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="content-meta small-thing">
          <div>
           <a class="content-type" data-track-action="Meta: Feature Type" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/search?tags=" href="/features/news-in-brief">
            NEWS IN BRIEF
           </a>
           <span class="content-published">
            December 9, 2013
           </span>
          </div>
          <div>
           <span class="content-issue">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Issue" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/issue/4950/" href="/issue/4950/">
             Vol 49 Issue 50
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="content-tags">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/business" href="/tag/business">
             Business
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/local" href="/tag/local">
             Local
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/holidays" href="/tag/holidays">
             Holidays
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <div class="article-share-tools share-container">
           <div class="share-tools share-widget" data-share-description="FAIRFAX, MNClutching a jagged hacksaw while staring unblinkingly from his black ski mask, a terrifying figure has reportedly been selling dead trees to passersby in the Fairfax Middle School parking lot for two weeks, sources confirmed Monday." data-share-image="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2450/1/16x9/1200.jpg" data-share-redirect-url="http://www.theonion.com/fb-close" data-share-title="Terrifying Man Selling Dead Trees Out Of Middle School Parking Lot" data-share-url="http://www.theonion.com/r/34783">
            <a class="share-facebook button" data-action="Facebook share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Facebook" href="#" target="_blank" title="Share via Facebook">
             <i class="fa fa-facebook fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-twitter button" data-action="Twitter share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Twitter" href="#" title="Share via Twitter">
             <i class="fa fa-twitter fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-mail button" data-action="Email share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Email" href="#" title="Share via Email">
             <i class="fa fa-envelope fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="dfp dfp-slot-article-button" data-ad-unit="article-button" data-targeting='{"dfp_pagetype": "article", "dfp_content_id": 34783}'>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="large-thing content-main">
          <div class="content-text">
           <div>
            <p>
             FAIRFAX, MNClutching a jagged hacksaw while staring unblinkingly from his black ski mask, a terrifying figure has reportedly been selling dead trees to passersby in the Fairfax Middle School parking lot for two weeks, sources confirmed Monday. Looking for a tree? the hulking brute of a man said while pacing behind local residents as they traversed row upon row of evergreen cadavers, occasionally stopping to prop up a frozen trees corpse to allow visitors to gape at its lifeless form. Like this one? Let me just cut off the bottom of its trunk for you real quick. Sources confirmed that the fearsome beast then dragged the dead body of a pine tree to a nearby car, grunted audibly as he bound it tightly to the automobiles roof with a length of twine, and then tried to sell onlookers a grisly, horrifying ring made from the severed, intertwined limbs of several gruesomely butchered firs.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
